ProseMirror" contenteditable="true" style="width: 775px;" translate="no"><h1><span>Tic-Tac-Toe AI Game</span></h1><p><span>Welcome to the Tic-Tac-Toe AI Game! This is a modern and interactive twist on the classic Tic-Tac-Toe game, featuring various levels of AI difficulty, player score tracking, and a sleek graphical interface.</span></p><h2><span>Features</span></h2><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span><strong>Graphical Interface</strong></span><span>: Built using the iGraphics library for a visually appealing experience.</span></p></li><li><p><span><strong>Multiplayer Mode</strong></span><span>: Play with a friend in two-player mode.</span></p></li><li><p><span><strong>AI Mode</strong></span><span>: Challenge yourself against the computer with three difficulty levels:</span></p><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>Easy</span></p></li><li><p><span>Medium</span></p></li><li><p><span>Hard</span></p></li></ul></li><li><p><span><strong>Unique Gameplay</strong></span><span>: Unlike traditional Tic-Tac-Toe, this game features </span><span><strong>four 3x3 boards</strong></span><span>, adding a layer of complexity and strategy. In AI mode, the board the player moves on determines the board where the AI will make its move, creating a dynamic and challenging experience.</span></p></li><li><p><span><strong>Scoreboard</strong></span><span>: Save and display top scores of players.</span></p></li><li><p><span><strong>Sound Effects</strong></span><span>: Enjoy background music and sound effects during gameplay.</span></p></li><li><p><span><strong>Settings and Rules</strong></span><span>: Easily access game settings and rules for better understanding.</span></p></li></ul><h2><span>Installation</span></h2><h3><span>Prerequisites</span></h3><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>A Windows-based system.</span></p></li><li><p><span>A C++ compiler (e.g., GCC, MinGW).</span></p></li><li><p><span>The </span><code><span>iGraphics</span></code><span> library installed on your system.</span></p></li></ul><h3><span>Steps</span></h3><ol data-spread="false" start="1"><li><p><span>Clone this repository:</span></p><div class="cm-editor ͼ1 ͼ3 ͼ4 ͼ1o ͼ2a" data-is-code-block-view="true" contenteditable="false"><div class="cm-announced" aria-live="polite"></div><div tabindex="-1" class="cm-scroller"><div spellcheck="false" autocorrect="off" autocapitalize="off" translate="no" contenteditable="true" class="cm-content" role="textbox" aria-multiline="true" data-language="shell" style="tab-size: 4;"><div class="cm-line"><span class="ͼ1r">git</span> clone https://github.com/your-username/tic-tac-toe-ai.git</div></div><div class="cm-layer cm-layer-above cm-cursorLayer" aria-hidden="true" style="z-index: 150; animation-duration: 1200ms;"><div class="cm-cursor cm-cursor-primary" style="left: 6px; top: 5px; height: 19px;"></div></div><div class="cm-layer cm-selectionLayer" aria-hidden="true" style="z-index: -2;"></div></div></div></li><li><p><span>Navigate to the project directory:</span></p><div class="cm-editor ͼ1 ͼ3 ͼ4 ͼ1o ͼ2b" data-is-code-block-view="true" contenteditable="false"><div class="cm-announced" aria-live="polite"></div><div tabindex="-1" class="cm-scroller"><div spellcheck="false" autocorrect="off" autocapitalize="off" translate="no" contenteditable="true" class="cm-content" role="textbox" aria-multiline="true" data-language="shell" style="tab-size: 4;"><div class="cm-line"><span class="ͼ1r">cd</span> tic-tac-toe-ai</div></div><div class="cm-layer cm-layer-above cm-cursorLayer" aria-hidden="true" style="z-index: 150; animation-duration: 1200ms;"><div class="cm-cursor cm-cursor-primary" style="left: 6px; top: 5px; height: 19px;"></div></div><div class="cm-layer cm-selectionLayer" aria-hidden="true" style="z-index: -2;"></div></div></div></li><li><p><span>Compile the code:</span></p><div class="cm-editor ͼ1 ͼ3 ͼ4 ͼ1o ͼ2c" data-is-code-block-view="true" contenteditable="false"><div class="cm-announced" aria-live="polite"></div><div tabindex="-1" class="cm-scroller"><div spellcheck="false" autocorrect="off" autocapitalize="off" translate="no" contenteditable="true" class="cm-content" role="textbox" aria-multiline="true" data-language="shell" style="tab-size: 4;"><div class="cm-line">g<span class="ͼ1w">+</span><span class="ͼ1w">+</span> iMain.cpp <span class="ͼ1r">-o</span> TicTacToe <span class="ͼ1r">-lgraphics</span></div></div><div class="cm-layer cm-layer-above cm-cursorLayer" aria-hidden="true" style="z-index: 150; animation-duration: 1200ms;"><div class="cm-cursor cm-cursor-primary" style="left: 6px; top: 5px; height: 19px;"></div></div><div class="cm-layer cm-selectionLayer" aria-hidden="true" style="z-index: -2;"></div></div></div></li><li><p><span>Run the executable:</span></p><div class="cm-editor ͼ1 ͼ3 ͼ4 ͼ1o ͼ2d" data-is-code-block-view="true" contenteditable="false"><div class="cm-announced" aria-live="polite"></div><div tabindex="-1" class="cm-scroller"><div spellcheck="false" autocorrect="off" autocapitalize="off" translate="no" contenteditable="true" class="cm-content" role="textbox" aria-multiline="true" data-language="shell" style="tab-size: 4;"><div class="cm-line">./TicTacToe</div></div><div class="cm-layer cm-layer-above cm-cursorLayer" aria-hidden="true" style="z-index: 150; animation-duration: 1200ms;"><div class="cm-cursor cm-cursor-primary" style="left: 6px; top: 5px; height: 19px;"></div></div><div class="cm-layer cm-selectionLayer" aria-hidden="true" style="z-index: -2;"></div></div></div></li></ol><h2><span>How to Play</span></h2><h3><span>Main Menu</span></h3><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span><strong>Start Game</strong></span><span>: Begin a new game by selecting either multiplayer or AI mode.</span></p></li><li><p><span><strong>Settings</strong></span><span>: Configure sound and other game options.</span></p></li><li><p><span><strong>Rules</strong></span><span>: View the game rules.</span></p></li></ul><h3><span>Gameplay</span></h3><ol data-spread="false" start="1"><li><p><span>Choose a mode (Player vs. Player or Player vs. AI).</span></p></li><li><p><span>In AI mode, select a difficulty level.</span></p></li><li><p><span>Play the game by clicking on the grid to place your symbol (</span><code><span>X</span></code><span> or </span><code><span>O</span></code><span>).</span></p></li><li><p><span>Navigate between the four 3x3 boards strategically. The AI will make its move on the board corresponding to your move, enhancing the complexity and fun.</span></p></li><li><p><span>The first player to get three in a row (horizontally, vertically, or diagonally) on any board wins!</span></p></li><li><p><span>Scores are saved automatically after the game.</span></p></li></ol><h2><span>File Structure</span></h2><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span><strong>iMain.cpp</strong></span><span>: The main source code for the game.</span></p></li><li><p><span><strong>resources/</strong></span><span>: Contains game assets like images and sound files.</span></p></li><li><p><span><strong>topScores.txt</strong></span><span>: Stores the top scores.</span></p></li></ul><h2><span>Acknowledgments</span></h2><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>Developed using the </span><code><span>iGraphics</span></code><span> library.</span></p></li><li><p><span>Special thanks to all contributors and players.</span></p></li></ul><p><span>Enjoy playing Tic-Tac-Toe AI!</span></p><p><span class="text-token-text-tertiary dark:text-gray-500 pointer-events-none select-none ProseMirror-widget"
